These leagues are open to all players as long as they are 16 years of age or older. Each of these leagues are recreational in nature where the focus of the leagues are having fun along with player safety. Our men's, women's and adult mixed indoor leagues are more competitive than the Over 30 leagues, but there are no tryouts involved and players of all skill levels are welcome to join.</span></p><p class="brz-fw-lg-700 brz-fss-lg-px brz-fs-lg-19 brz-ft-google brz-text-lg-justify brz-fsft-lg-0 brz-fwdth-lg-100 brz-vfw-lg-400 brz-lh-lg-1_8 brz-ls-lg-0 brz-text-sm-center brz-tp-sm-empty brz-fs-sm-16 brz-fss-sm-px brz-fw-sm-700 brz-ls-sm-0 brz-lh-sm-1_6 brz-vfw-sm-400 brz-fwdth-sm-100 brz-fsft-sm-0 brz-fss-xs-px brz-fw-xs-700 brz-ls-xs-0 brz-lh-xs-1_8 brz-vfw-xs-400 brz-fwdth-xs-100 brz-fsft-xs-0 brz-tp-xs-empty brz-fs-xs-16 brz-tp-lg-empty brz-ff-fira_sans brz-css-bLMNw" data-generated-css="brz-css-fEIyf" data-uniq-id="jzKvQ"><span class="brz-cp-color2" style="text-shadow: rgb(255, 255, 255) 1px 2px 4px;
